</span><span id="L-913"><a href="#L-913"><span class="linenos">913</span></a>                <span class="n">obj</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">dcoi</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">type_id</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">afs</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">type_id</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">obj_info</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">ObjectInfoFields</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">object_</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">value</span><span class="p">]))</span>
</span><span id="L-914"><a href="#L-914"><span class="linenos">914</span></a>            <span class="k">else</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="L-915"><a href="#L-915"><span class="linenos">915</span></a>                <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="ne">RuntimeError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;Unknown type_id&#39;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="L-916"><a href="#L-916"><span class="linenos">916</span></a>        
</span><span id="L-917"><a href="#L-917"><span class="linenos">917</span></a>        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">objects_db</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">object_id</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">obj</span>
</span><span id="L-918"><a href="#L-918"><span class="linenos">918</span></a>        <span class="n">id_</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">id</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">obj</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="L-919"><a href="#L-919"><span class="linenos">919</span></a>        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">objects_ids</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">object_id</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">id_</span>
</span><span id="L-920"><a href="#L-920"><span class="linenos">920</span></a>        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">objects_ids_by_id</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">id_</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">object_id</span>
</span><span id="L-921"><a href="#L-921"><span class="linenos">921</span></a>        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">ResultExistence</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">Tuple</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nb">int</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Any</span><span class="p">]](</span><span class="kc">True</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">object_id</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">obj</span><span class="p">))</span>
</span><span id="L-922"><a href="#L-922"><span class="linenos">922</span></a>    
</span><span id="L-923"><a href="#L-923"><span class="linenos">923</span></a>    <span class="n">doi</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">deserialize_obj_impl</span>
</span><span id="L-924"><a href="#L-924"><span class="linenos">924</span></a>
</span><span id="L-925"><a href="#L-925"><span class="linenos">925</span></a>    <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">deserialize_obj</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">obj_info</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">Tuple</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">-&gt;</span> <span class="n">ResultExistence</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">Tuple</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nb">int</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Any</span><span class="p">]]:</span>
</span><span id="L-926"><a href="#L-926"><span class="linenos">926</span></a>        <span class="k">with</span> <span class="n">DisableGC</span><span class="p">():</span>
